# Apache Beam Pipeline Runner Translation Layer

## Your Task

Find all Java source files in apache/beam under runners/core-java/ and runners/core-construction-java/ that translate a Beam pipeline graph into runner-specific execution primitives. Identify: the PipelineTranslator interface, the TransformHierarchy walker, the PTransformOverride mechanism, the ExecutableStagePayload construction, and the BoundedSource/UnboundedSource adapter classes. For each file report its path and key class name.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossorg domain.

packages, primarily located in sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk (for the core SDK) and runners directories (for runner-specific implementations).\\n\\n## Core Translation Infrastructure\\n\\n**PipelineTranslation System**: The `PipelineTranslation` class (sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/PipelineTranslation.java) is the central class that converts Beam Pipeline objects to/from Runner API protocol buffers. It works with `SdkComponents` (sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/SdkComponents.java) which manages the registration and lookup of coders, windowing strategies, and other SDK components.\\n\\n**TransformHierarchy Walker**: The `TransformHierarchy` class (sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/runners/TransformHierarchy.java) represents the hierarchical structure of transforms in a pipeline. The TransformHierarchy.Node inner class walks the pipeline tree, allowing traversal and manipulation of the transform graph.\\n\\n**PTransformOverride Mechanism**: The override mechanism is implemented through:\\n- `PTransformOverride` interface (sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/runners/PTransformOverride.java) - defines how to detect and replace transforms\\n- `PTransformOverrideFactory` (sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/runners/PTransformOverrideFactory.java) - factory interface for creating overrides\\n- Concrete implementations like `SingleInputOutputOverrideFactory`, `SplittableParDo`, and `DeduplicatedFlattenFactory` provide specific transform replacements\\n- Support utilities: `PTransformMatchers` (matches transform patterns), `PTransformReplacements` (handles replacement logic), `ReplacementOutputs` (maps output connections)\\n\\n**ExecutableStagePayload Construction**: The `ExecutableStageTranslation` class (sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/ExecutableStageTranslation.java) manages conversion of ExecutableStages to/from proto payloads. The `ExecutableStage` interface (sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/graph/ExecutableStage.java) and its implementation `ImmutableExecutableStage` (sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/graph/ImmutableExecutableStage.java) represent executable units. Supporting reference classes like `SideInputReference`, `TimerReference`, and `UserStateReference` represent the components within ExecutableStagePayload.\\n\\n**BoundedSource/UnboundedSource Adapters**: \\n- Base classes: `BoundedSource` and `UnboundedSource` (in sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/io/)\\n- Adapter implementations: `UnboundedReadFromBoundedSource` (sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/UnboundedReadFromBoundedSource.java) converts BoundedSource to UnboundedSource\\n- `BoundedReadFromUnboundedSource` (sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/io/BoundedReadFromUnboundedSource.java) does the reverse\\n- `ReadTranslation` (sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/ReadTranslation.java) handles translation of Read transforms to/from proto format, managing both bounded and unbounded sources\\n\\n## Transform-Specific Translators\\n\\nThe system includes specific translator classes for major transforms:\\n- `ParDoTranslation` for ParDo transforms\\n- `CombineTranslation` for Combine operations\\n- `GroupByKeyTranslation` for GroupByKey operations\\n- `FlattenTranslator` for Flatten operations\\n- Coder translators: `CoderTranslator`, `CoderTranslators`, and `CoderTranslation`\\n\\n## Graph Analysis and Fusion\\n\\nFor runner optimization, the system includes:\\n- `QueryablePipeline` for graph traversal and querying\\n- `GreedyPipelineFuser` and `GreedyStageFuser` for stage fusion\\n- `PipelineValidator` for validating ExecutableStagePayload content\\n- Graph optimization via `ProtoOverrides` for proto-based transform overrides\\n\\n## FnExecution Runner Support\\n\\nThe runners/java-fn-execution/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/runners/fnexecution/translation/ package contains:\\n- `PipelineTranslatorUtils` for shared translation utilities\\n- `BatchSideInputHandlerFactory` and `StreamingSideInputHandlerFactory` for managing side inputs during execution\\n\\nThis architecture enables the flexible translation of high-level Beam pipelines into runner-specific execution primitives while maintaining abstraction boundaries and supporting multiple execution models.\"\n}\n",

that converts Beam Pipeline objects to/from Runner API protocol buffers. It works with `SdkComponents` (sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/SdkComponents.java) which manages the registration and lookup of coders, windowing strategies, and other SDK components.\\n\\n**TransformHierarchy Walker**: The `TransformHierarchy` class (sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/runners/TransformHierarchy.java) represents the hierarchical structure of transforms in a pipeline. The TransformHierarchy.Node inner class walks the pipeline tree, allowing traversal and manipulation of the transform graph.\\n\\n**PTransformOverride Mechanism**: The override mechanism is implemented through:\\n- `PTransformOverride` interface (sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/runners/PTransformOverride.java) - defines how to detect and replace transforms\\n- `PTransformOverrideFactory` (sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/runners/PTransformOverrideFactory.java) - factory interface for creating overrides\\n- Concrete implementations like `SingleInputOutputOverrideFactory`, `SplittableParDo`, and `DeduplicatedFlattenFactory` provide specific transform replacements\\n- Support utilities: `PTransformMatchers` (matches transform patterns), `PTransformReplacements` (handles replacement logic), `ReplacementOutputs` (maps output connections)\\n\\n**ExecutableStagePayload Construction**: The `ExecutableStageTranslation` class (sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/ExecutableStageTranslation.java) manages conversion of ExecutableStages to/from proto payloads. Adapters**: \\n- Base classes: `BoundedSource` and `UnboundedSource` (in sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/io/)\\n- Adapter implementations: `UnboundedReadFromBoundedSource`
